							<input type="checkbox" class="hidden" id="pages-nav-hamburger">
							<section id="elastic-docs-v3">
	<h1>Build your search queries</h1>

		<p class="applies applies-block">
		
		<span class="applicable-info" data-tippy-content="Available on Elastic&nbsp;Cloud&nbsp;Serverless unless otherwise specified.">
			<span class="applicable-name">Serverless</span>
			
			<span class="applicable-meta applicable-meta-ga">
			</span>
		</span>
		<span class="applicable-info" data-tippy-content="Available on Elastic&nbsp;Stack unless otherwise specified.

If this functionality is unavailable or behaves differently when deployed on ECH, ECE, ECK, or a self-managed installation, it will be indicated on the page.">
			<span class="applicable-name">Stack</span>
			
			<span class="applicable-meta applicable-meta-ga">
			</span>
		</span>

		</p>
	<div class="admonition tip">
	<div class="admonition-header">
		<span class="admonition-title">Tip</span>
	</div>
	<div class="admonition-content"><p>This page is focused on the search use case. For an overview of Elastic query languages for every use case, refer to the <a href="/docs/explore-analyze/query-filter/languages" hx-select-oob="#main-container" preload="mousedown">complete overview</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<p>Once you know which <a href="/docs/solutions/search/search-approaches" hx-select-oob="#content-container,#toc-nav" preload="mousedown">search approaches</a> you need to use, you can start building and testing your search queries. Elasticsearch provides several query languages to help you express your search logic.</p>
<div class="table-wrapper">
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Interface</th>
<th>Endpoint</th>
<th>Description</th>
<th>Best for</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a href="/docs/explore-analyze/query-filter/languages/querydsl" hx-select-oob="#main-container" preload="mousedown"><strong>Query DSL</strong></a></td>
<td><a href="/docs/solutions/search/the-search-api" hx-select-oob="#content-container,#toc-nav" preload="mousedown"><code>_search</code></a></td>
<td>Original, JSON-based query language native to Elasticsearch. Powerful but complex syntax.</td>
<td>Full-text and semantic search queries</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/docs/solutions/search/esql-for-search" hx-select-oob="#content-container,#toc-nav" preload="mousedown"><strong>ES|QL</strong></a></td>
<td><code>_query</code></td>
<td>Fast, SQL-like language with piped syntax, built on new compute architecture.</td>
<td>Filtering, analysis, aggregations</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/docs/solutions/search/retrievers-overview" hx-select-oob="#content-container,#toc-nav" preload="mousedown"><strong>Retrievers</strong></a></td>
<td><code>_search</code></td>
<td>Modern <code>_search</code> API syntax focused on composability.</td>
<td>Building complex search pipelines, especially those using semantic search. Required for <a href="/docs/solutions/search/ranking/semantic-reranking" hx-select-oob="#content-container,#toc-nav" preload="mousedown">semantic reranking</a>.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<p>These query languages are complementary, not mutually exclusive. You can use different query languages for different parts of your application, based on your specific needs. This flexibility allows you to gradually adopt newer interfaces as your requirements evolve.</p>
<div class="admonition note">
	<div class="admonition-header">
		<span class="admonition-title">Note</span>
	</div>
	<div class="admonition-content"><p>You can use the <a href="https://www.elastic.co/docs/api/doc/elasticsearch" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Elasticsearch REST APIs</a> to search your data using any HTTP client, including the <a href="/docs/solutions/search/site-or-app/clients" hx-select-oob="#content-container,#toc-nav" preload="mousedown">Elasticsearch client libraries</a>, or directly in <a href="/docs/explore-analyze/query-filter/tools/console" hx-select-oob="#main-container" preload="mousedown">Console</a>. You can also run searches using <a href="/docs/explore-analyze/discover" hx-select-oob="#main-container" preload="mousedown">Discover</a> in the UI.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="admonition tip">
	<div class="admonition-header">
		<span class="admonition-title">Tip</span>
	</div>
	<div class="admonition-content"><p>Try our hands-on <a href="/docs/solutions/search/get-started/quickstarts" hx-select-oob="#content-container,#toc-nav" preload="mousedown">quickstart guides</a> to get started, or check out our <a href="https://github.com/elastic/elasticsearch-labs/tree/main/notebooks#readme" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Python notebooks</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>

</section>
